<rating>4</rating>< review>
Excellent, motivated trainers and friendly members.
I was visiting from Canada this week and rather than use the teeny hotel gym I, tried 2 morning classes at LA Fitness because it was near my hotel.  The drop in was $15/day (not cheap but reasonable).  Jenn's Thursday class and the Spin leader on Friday were fantastic - both leaders made me feel welcome as a new participant, and the other members were friendly and clearly have a great rapport with each other.  Both classes were well formatted and allowed participants to modify exercises, weight, etc.
The only reason I gave it a 4/5 is because there were no wipes or spray bottles to clean the equipment/mats etc. This should be a no brainer.</review>

< review>
My car was making a choppy/stuttering sound and I was due for an oil change so I brought it into service. Jason was my service advisor and I told him my concerns with the engine/loud sound. I also asked him to check for anything else that I needed to change (i.e. fuel filters) but he told me that MINI usually has good fuel filters but that he would still advise service to check it anyways. Jason also assisted me with the car loaner department and when I expressed concern about when I should drive back or how long my car would take, he reassured me that he would keep me updated on the progress and to keep the loaner car as long as I had needed during service. Later Jason texted me and said that we had a faulty thermostat and the water pump pulley was missing a chunk. His explanation was detailed and very helpful for me to understand, as I don't know much about cars. The next day I got a message saying that my car was ready but Jason told me to wait another day because he wanted to make sure that the oil change was done in addition to the other work. He was very helpful throughout the whole process and I would recommend him as a service advisor to anyone who has a MINI.</review>

<username>andrea lyn< /username><UserId.>104196090569471677126</UserId.><Pictures>None< /Pictures>< text>
I couldn't wait to get into my new Mini. Those little cars are so cute and they're made by BMW - must be of good quality, or so I thought.
All the cars come with leather interiors and then there's the option for those sharp looking black enamel spoke wheels.  I ended up getting the Clubman model - it's more spacious than the Cooper and the ride is smoother.  I was happy with my little car ... for about 4 1/2 months, when it needed a brake pad replacement and, as it turned out, a front wheel alignment as well.
Not quite 6 months later, the brake pads needed replacement for the second time .... this is what I have to look forward to ??  I'm so regretful that I didn't go back to Honda - never had problems with those cars.
Honestly, in all my years of driving any make, style, used or new car,  I never had to have the brake pads replaced even once in less than a year.
When I questioned the service manager about the brake pads needing replacement so soon and so frequently, the answer I got was,
"Well, they're a sportier car so the brake pads tend to be a little softer."
Ok ... whatever.
I was also asked:
"Do you drive in a lot of stop and go traffic ?"
Really ??  (this is Los Angeles) Nah, not much.
I'm sorry but brake pads are absolutely essential for the safety of the driver, the passengers and, everyone else on the road.  How does a big name car manufacturer skimp on something as vital as brake pads and be okay with it ??
But if you're really bent on investing in one of those cute little Minis - PLEASE ! buy the extended warranty ... you're gonna need it !< /text>

< review>
This is the worst service experience I have had out of 4 or 5 MINI dealerships I have taken my MINI to for servicing. My contact was Anthony and I was given a loaner car, as requested.
1. Checking in went fine. Driving my car right up to the service door was odd because the parking lot was cramped. I squeezed my MINI through the cars no problem, but a larger vehicle definitely would not have made it through.
2. They charged a $500 diagnosing fee right off the bat.
3. After checking in, I waited almost an hour for the loaner car. That has never happened at other dealerships.
4. After getting home, which is a 45 minute drive, I called to have my husband added as a driver to the loaner car. The first answer I got was that we had to come back in to let them photo copy his driver's license. Sending it over email was not an option. I called the car loan person directly to confirm this and left a detailed message, asking her to call back. In the meantime, we made the 45 minute drive, rushing to make it before their closing time. When we get there, the car loan person was sitting right at her desk. Apparently, as long as my husband is on the same insurance, we were fine. We did not have to provide them with his driver's license. Well, thanks for not calling me back to let me know.
5. I provided Anthony with a quote from Firestone for suggested repairs. The prices he gave me the next day were considerably pricier than the Firestone quotes, which I suppose is a given since this is a MINI dealership. They did not even attempt to match Firestone's quote.
6. There is a class action lawsuit regarding known defects in the transmission. Basically they sold the cars knowing the transmission was faulty. But the dealership would only replace my "internal failure" transmission if I paid almost $11k. My car is not even worth that anymore.
7. We are now in the market for a new car which will NOT be a MINI or BMW.< /review>

March 4, 2016

On this time of regular check and repair of my BMW X-3
(at BMW of Monrovia, 1425-1451 South Mountain Ave. Monrovia, CA 91016)

This time of regular check was so far good as on the return drive from the service to my house.

But this time repair was very disappointed.
Reason is that both left and right LED rear tail light housings were replaced and charged $792.75 (including labor charge but not including tax).
When I visited at the service for the regular check and the repair, I told and requested the service person to do regular check and to fix only left rear light which was not turned on.
Then, the service person phoned and explained after they checked my X-3 that left rear LED light bulb itself was not be able to be replaced. Instead, whole assemble of rear LED light housings of not only left but also of right should be replaced.
I didn‚Äôt have any choice avoid this expensive and uncomfortable repair charge.

The points which I am very unhappy are ;

(1)	This time problem is definitely part defects (or parts not reliable). Current technology of LED light bulb is very reliable and long life. And These LED light whole housings are the original ones.  Why should I pay for it?
(2)	This LED housing design was not customer oriented. Because, Customers have to replace whole housing of both left and right instead of left LED light bulb it self. Why BMW (as one of the most honorable automobile manufacturer) had designed such customer uncomfortable one?

If you have any explanation of the reason why or any excuse against my points stated above, please send me an e-mail.
Also, if you refund the charge ($792.75), I am very comfortable.  Please let me know.

Noboru kasai
1641 Oakhaven Drive Arcadia CA, 91006<//review>
